3. **Viral Sinusitis (2015):** In the same year, she was diagnosed with viral sinusitis.

4. **Full-time Employment (2018):** In 2018, she transitioned to full-time employment, with an increase in her BMI.

6. **Generalized Anxiety Disorder (2021):** She also reported symptoms of generalized anxiety disorder, with a GAD-7 score of 4.

7. **Streptococcal Sore Throat (2021):** In 2021, Luisa presented with a streptococcal sore throat.

8. **Current Status (2023):** As of the latest records in 2023, she has not reported any significant medical issues.

1. **Acute Viral Pharyngitis (2014):** In 2014, she was diagnosed with acute viral pharyngitis.

2. **Medication Review Due (2015):** In 2015, she had a medication review due and reported stress and social isolation.

3. **Viral Sinusitis (2015):** In the same year, she was diagnosed with viral sinusitis.

4. **Full-time Employment (2018):** In 2018, she transitioned to full-time employment, with an increase in her BMI.

5. **Prediabetes and Anemia (2021):** In 2021, Luisa was diagnosed with prediabetes and anemia, with increased glucose levels and a slightly elevated HbA1c.

6. **Generalized Anxiety Disorder (2021):** She also reported symptoms of generalized anxiety disorder, with a GAD-7 score of 4.

7. **Streptococcal Sore Throat (2021):** In 2021, Luisa presented with a streptococcal sore throat.

8. **Current Status (2023):** As of the latest records in 2023, she has not reported any significant medical issues.

**Treatment Course:**
Throughout her medical history, Luisa has received the following treatments and interventions:

1. **Immunizations:** She has consistently received influenza vaccinations.

2. **Medication Management:** Luisa has undergone medication reviews at various points in her medical history.

3. **Gynecological Treatment:** She received a medroxyprogesterone acetate injection in 2018, suggesting a form of birth control or hormonal management.

4. **COVID-19 Vaccination:** She received the SARS-COV-2 (COVID-19) vaccine in 2021.

5. **Basic Metabolic Panels:** Periodic basic metabolic panels have been conducted.

**Current Clinical Data:**
As of the latest records in 2023:

- Luisa's BMI is within a healthy range.
- She has reported no significant pain.
- Blood pressure, heart rate, and respiratory rate are within normal limits.
- She no longer smokes tobacco.
- Her HbA1c levels remain slightly elevated.
